Wenhua Road Night Market in Chiayi, Taiwan, is one of the well-known night markets in the city. Situated along Wenhua Road, it's a bustling spot loved by locals and tourists alike. Renowned for its diverse array of snacks and unique delicacies, this night market offers a wide range of Taiwanese cuisines such as stinky tofu, crispy fried chicken, pearl milk tea, and more, allowing visitors to savor authentic Taiwanese flavors. Additionally, the market features numerous stalls selling clothing, goods, and handicrafts, providing visitors with opportunities for shopping and browsing. Within the lively atmosphere of the night market, people can enjoy delicious food, experience the vibrant ambiance, and immerse themselves in the energetic nightlife culture of Taiwan.", '4 é¡†æ˜Ÿ
